@RequestMapping(value={"/showBio"})
    public String showBio(ModelMap model, @RequestParam String getCategory, @RequestParam String title,
            HttpServletRequest request, HttpSession session){

        List<Product> product = productDao.getProductsByCategory(getCategory);

        if(product.isEmpty()){
           model.put("productEmpty","No products Yet");

       }else if(product.size()>0 && product.size()<=1){

        owner = product.get(0).getOwner(); id = product.get(0).getId();

        model.put("product","<form action=\"/e-Farm/orderFromIndex\" id=\"myForm\" method=\"POST\" >\n" +

"                    <div class=\"panel-footer\">"+ publicLocal +"</div>\n" +

"                \n" +

"                   <div class=\"panel panel-primary\">\n" +
"                    <div class=\"panel-heading\">"+owner+"<input type=\"hidden\" value="+ id +" id=\"theId\" name=\"theId\" /></div>\n" +
"                    <div class=\"panel-body\"> <input type=\"hidden\" value="+owner+" id=\"theOwner\" name=\"theOwner\" /><img onclick=\"mySubmit()\" src=\"resources/images/veges.jpeg\" class=\"img-responsive\" style=\"width:100%\" alt=\"Image\"></div>\n" +
"                    <div class=\"panel-footer\">"+ publicLocal +"</div>\n" +
"                   </div> \n" +
"                </div>\n" +
"                \n" +
"               </form>  \n" +
"                <script>\n" +
"            function mySubmit() {\n" +
"\n" +
"                document.getElementById(\"myForm\").submit();\n" +
"            }\n" +
"        </script>");

        }else{

        model.put("tooManyProducts","You are not allowed to create more products");

       }
        byte[] ptext = title.getBytes(ISO_8859_1);
        String value = new String(ptext, UTF_8);
        model.put("title",value);
        model.put("c0","Άνοιξη");
        model.put("c1","Καλοκαίρι");
        model.put("c2","Φθινόπωρο");
        model.put("c3","Χειμώνας");
        model.put("b0","Βότανα");
        model.put("b1","Γάλατα");
        model.put("b2","Δημητριακά");
        model.put("b3","Κήπος");
        model.put("b4","Λαχανικά");
        model.put("b5","Ξηροί Καρποί");
        model.put("b6","Φρούτα");
        model.put("b7","Άλλα Βιολογικά Προϊόντα");
        return "bioHome";
    }
    // LAXANIKA - START
    @RequestMapping(value={"/showVeges"})
    public String showVeges(ModelMap model, @RequestParam String getCategory, @RequestParam String title,
            HttpServletRequest request, HttpSession session){

        List<Product> product = productDao.getProductsByCategory(getCategory);

        if(product.isEmpty()){
           model.put("productEmpty","No products Yet");

       }else if(product.size()>0 && product.size()<=1){

        model.put("c2","Φθινόπωρο");
        model.put("c3","Χειμώνας");
        return "laxanikaHome";
    }

    @RequestMapping(value={"/showProducts"}, method = RequestMethod.POST , produces = "text/plain; charset=UTF-8")
    public String showProducts(ModelMap model, @RequestParam String getCategory,@RequestParam String getSubCategory,
            @RequestParam String title , HttpServletRequest request, HttpSession session) throws UnsupportedEncodingException{
        HttpHeaders responseHeaders = new HttpHeaders();
        responseHeaders.add("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=UTF-8");
        StringHttpMessageConverter stringHttpMessageConverter = new StringHttpMessageConverter(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);

        List<Product> product = productDao.getProductsBySubCategory(getCategory, getSubCategory);

        if(product.isEmpty()){
           model.put("productEmpty","No products Yet");

       }else if(product.size()>0 && product.size()<=1){

        owner = product.get(0).getOwner(); id = product.get(0).getId();
        publicLocal = product.get(0).getPublicLocal();
        model.put("product","<form action=\"/e-Farm/orderFromIndex\" id=\"myForm\" method=\"POST\" >\n" +
"                <div class=\"col-sm-4\">\n" +
"                   <div class=\"panel panel-primary\">\n" +
"                    <div class=\"panel-heading\">"+owner+"<input type=\"hidden\" value="+ id +" id=\"theId\" name=\"theId\" /></div>\n" +
"                    <div class=\"panel-body\"> <input type=\"hidden\" value="+owner+" id=\"theOwner\" name=\"theOwner\" /><img onclick=\"mySubmit()\" src=\"resources/images/veges.jpeg\" class=\"img-responsive\" style=\"width:100%\" alt=\"Image\"></div>\n" +

        String value = new String(ptext, UTF_8);
        model.put("title",value);
        model.put("c0","Άνοιξη");
        model.put("c1","Καλοκαίρι");
        model.put("c2","Φθινόπωρο");
        model.put("c3","Χειμώνας");

        model.put("g3","Γάλα Ρυζιού");
        model.put("g4","Γάλα Κάναβης");
        model.put("g5","Γάλα Καρύδας");
        model.put("g6","Γάλα Σόγιας");
        model.put("g7","Γάλα Φουντουκιού");
        model.put("g8","Γιαούρτια");
        model.put("g9","Τυριά");

        return "products";
    }

    @RequestMapping(value={"/showBioProducts"}, method = RequestMethod.POST , produces = "text/plain; charset=UTF-8")
    public String showBioProducts(ModelMap model, @RequestParam String getCategory,@RequestParam String getBio,
            @RequestParam String title , HttpServletRequest request, HttpSession session) throws UnsupportedEncodingException{
        HttpHeaders responseHeaders = new HttpHeaders();
        responseHeaders.add("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=UTF-8");
        StringHttpMessageConverter stringHttpMessageConverter = new StringHttpMessageConverter(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);

        List<Product> product = productDao.getProductsByBioCategory(getCategory, getBio);

        if(product.isEmpty()){
           model.put("productEmpty","No products Yet");

       }else if(product.size()>0 && product.size()<=1){

        owner = product.get(0).getOwner(); id = product.get(0).getId();
        publicLocal = product.get(0).getPublicLocal();
        model.put("product","<form action=\"/e-Farm/orderFromIndex\" id=\"myForm\" method=\"POST\" >\n" +

"                    <div class=\"panel-heading\">"+owner+"<input type=\"hidden\" value="+ id +" id=\"theId\" name=\"theId\" /></div>\n" +

        byte[] ptext = title.getBytes(ISO_8859_1);
        String value = new String(ptext, UTF_8);
        model.put("title",value);
        model.put("c0","Άνοιξη");
        model.put("c1","Καλοκαίρι");
        model.put("c2","Φθινόπωρο");
        model.put("c3","Χειμώνας");
        return "products";
    }



    //LAXANIKA - END

    @RequestMapping(value={"/showFruits"})
    public String showFruits(ModelMap model, @RequestParam String getCategory, @RequestParam String title,
            HttpServletRequest request, HttpSession session) throws UnsupportedEncodingException{

        List<Product> product = productDao.getProductsByCategory(getCategory);

        if(product.isEmpty()){
           model.put("productEmpty","No products Yet");

       }else if(product.size()>0 && product.size()<=1){

        owner = product.get(0).getOwner(); id = product.get(0).getId();
        publicLocal = product.get(0).getPublicLocal();
        model.put("product","<form action=\"/e-Farm/orderFromIndex\" id=\"myForm\" method=\"POST\" >\n" +

"                   </div> \n" +
"                </div>\n" +

    @RequestMapping(value={"/showCereals"})
    public String showDimitriaka(ModelMap model, @RequestParam String getCategory, @RequestParam String title,
            HttpServletRequest request, HttpSession session){

        List<Product> product = productDao.getProductsByCategory(getCategory);

        if(product.isEmpty()){
           model.put("productEmpty","No products Yet");

       }else if(product.size()>0 && product.size()<=1){

    @RequestMapping(value={"/showNuts"})
    public String showNuts(ModelMap model, @RequestParam String getCategory, @RequestParam String title,
            HttpServletRequest request, HttpSession session){

        List<Product> product = productDao.getProductsByCategory(getCategory);

        if(product.isEmpty()){
           model.put("productEmpty","No products Yet");

       }else if(product.size()>0 && product.size()<=1){

        owner = product.get(0).getOwner(); id = product.get(0).getId();
        publicLocal = product.get(0).getPublicLocal();

    @RequestMapping(value={"/showHerbs"})
    public String showHerbs(ModelMap model, @RequestParam String getCategory, @RequestParam String title,
            HttpServletRequest request, HttpSession session){

        List<Product> product = productDao.getProductsByCategory(getCategory);

        if(product.isEmpty()){
           model.put("productEmpty","No products Yet");

       }else if(product.size()>0 && product.size()<=1){

    @RequestMapping(value={"/showDairy"})
    public String showDairy(ModelMap model, @RequestParam String getCategory, @RequestParam String title,
            HttpServletRequest request, HttpSession session){

        List<Product> product = productDao.getProductsByCategory(getCategory);

        if(product.isEmpty()){
           model.put("productEmpty","No products Yet");

       }else if(product.size()>0 && product.size()<=1){

        publicLocal = product.get(0).getPublicLocal();

    }




    @RequestMapping(value={"/showGarden"})
    public String showKipos(ModelMap model, @RequestParam String getCategory, @RequestParam String title,
            HttpServletRequest request, HttpSession session){

        List<Product> product = productDao.getProductsByCategory(getCategory);

        if(product.isEmpty()){
           model.put("productEmpty","No products Yet");

       }else if(product.size()>0 && product.size()<=1){

        owner = product.get(0).getOwner(); id = product.get(0).getId();
        publicLocal = product.get(0).getPublicLocal();
        model.put("product","<form action=\"/e-Farm/orderFromIndex\" id=\"myForm\" method=\"POST\" >\n" +

"                   </div> \n" +
